<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: YOU HAVE READ THE LAW REGARDING SPOUSAL ABUSE; IS THAT CORRECT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND WERE YOU AWARE OF THE LAW AS IT STOOD IN 1989?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WHAT DUTY, IF ANY, UNDER THE LAW, DID YOU HAVE TO ARREST THIS DEFENDANT ON JANUARY 1, 1989?
<P>
<B>MR. COCHRAN:</B> I'M GOING TO OBJECT TO THE FORM OF THAT QUESTION, YOUR HONOR.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> OVERRULED.
<P>
<B>THE WITNESS:</B> UNDER 273.5 OF THE PENAL CODE AND 13700 OF THE PENAL CODE, I SHALL ARREST THAT PERSON. THERE IS NO IF, ANDS, BUTS ABOUT IT, WILLS OR MAYS, I SHALL ARREST THE DEFENDANT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU ARE REQUIRED UNDER THE LAW UNDER THESE CIRCUMSTANCES TO ARREST?
<P>
<B>A:</B> UNDER THE PENAL CODE AND MY DEPARTMENT POLICY, ABSOLUTELY, I HAVE TO ARREST THAT PERSON.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU TOLD MR. COCHRAN A MOMENT AGO THAT YOU DID NOT EXAMINE THE DEFENDANT UP CLOSE; IS THAT RIGHT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> JUST WITHIN ABOUT A FOOT OF THE FENCE BETWEEN US.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> HAD HE NOT RUN AWAY, WOULD YOU HAVE HAD AN OPPORTUNITY TO EXAMINE HIM?
<P>
<B>MR. COCHRAN:</B> OBJECT TO THE FORM OF THAT QUESTION, YOUR HONOR; ARGUMENTATIVE.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> OVERRULED. YOU CAN ANSWER THE QUESTION.
<P>
<B>THE WITNESS:</B> YES, I WOULD HAVE HAD A CHANCE TO EXAMINE HIM THOROUGHLY HAD HE NOT FLED THE SCENE.

<P>
<B>A:</B> ABSOLUTELY.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> THAT IS THE SITUATION. YOU WEREN'T INTERESTED IN HIS WELFARE AT THAT POINT; IS THAT CORRECT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I COULD SEE HE WAS NOT INJURED.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU COULDN'T SEE ANYTHING -- STRIKE THAT.
YOU HAD MADE A DECISION AND THAT IS WHAT YOU WERE GOING TO CARRY OUT; ISN'T THAT RIGHT, OFFICER?
<P>
<B>A:</B> UNDER THE PENAL CODE AND DEPARTMENT POLICY, HE WAS GOING TO JAIL FOR 273.5.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> RIGHT. AND AS YOU SAID, IF THE OTHER OFFICERS HAD BEEN OUT THERE SEVEN OR EIGHT TIMES, ISN'T THAT THE SAME LAW THAT YOU WERE UNDER ON JANUARY 1ST?
<P>
<B>A:</B> EXACTLY.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> THAT WOULD MEAN THAT SINCE HE WASN'T ARRESTED, NOTHING HAPPENED LIKE THAT; ISN'T THAT CORRECT? THAT IS NOT WHAT THE LAW IS; ISN'T THAT CORRECT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NOT NECESSARILY.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> NOT NECESSARILY. BUT YOU DON'T KNOW, DO YOU?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I DON'T KNOW AND NEITHER DO YOU.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU DIDN'T BOTHER CHECKING, DID YOU?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU THOUGHT THE SERGEANT WOULD CHECK THAT, DIDN'T YOU?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I THOUGHT THE SERGEANT OR THE DETECTIVE THAT WAS HANDLING THE CASE WOULD CHECK THAT, YES.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU DON'T KNOW WHETHER OR NOT THEY CHECKED THAT OR NOT, DO YOU?
<P>
<B>A:</B> AS FAR AS I KNOW, I DON'T KNOW.

<P>
DIRECT EXAMINATION
<P>
BY MR. DARDEN:
<P>
<B>Q:</B> SIR, WERE YOU A POLICE OFFICER EMPLOYED BY THE LAPD ON JANUARY 3, 1989?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I WAS.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND WHAT WAS YOUR ASSIGNMENT AT THAT TIME?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I WAS ASSIGNED TO WEST L.A. DETECTIVES ASSIGNED TO THE CRIMES AGAINST PERSONS DETAIL.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DID THE CRIMES AGAINST PERSON DETAIL INCLUDE SPOUSAL BATTERY CASES?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, THEY DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. DID YOU RESPOND TO 360 NORTH ROCKINGHAM ON THE MORNING OF JANUARY 1, 1989?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO, I DID NOT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU WERE NOT A PATROL OFFICER AT THAT TIME?
<P>
<B>A:</B> THAT IS NOT -- I WAS NOT A PATROL OFFICER, NO.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND ON JANUARY 3, 1989, WERE YOU ASSIGNED A CASE INVOLVING NICOLE BROWN AND THIS DEFENDANT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I WAS.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. AND WHO ASSIGNED YOU THAT CASE, IF YOU RECALL?
<P>
<B>A:</B> MY SUPERVISOR WAS DETECTIVE SERGEANT GLENN VARNER.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND WHAT IS THE NORMAL PROCEDURE FOR A DETECTIVE IN WEST L.A. DIVISION AFTER A CASE IS ASSIGNED TO THEM?
<P>
<B>A:</B> WELL, THIS CASE -- AFTER IT WAS ASSIGNED TO ME, MY SUPERVISOR EXPLAINED TO ME WHAT I SHOULD DO WITH IT AND ADJUDICATE IT AS SOON AS POSSIBLE BY INTERVIEWING THE VICTIM AND THE DEFENDANT, IF POSSIBLE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DID YOU INTERVIEW THE DEFENDANT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU INTERVIEW HIM IN PERSON?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO, I DID NOT. I INTERVIEWED HIM OVER THE TELEPHONE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DO YOU RECALL WHO CALLED WHO?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES. I PHONED THE RESIDENCE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> HOW MANY TIMES DID YOU PHONE THE RESIDENCE BEFORE YOU FINALLY SPOKE TO THE DEFENDANT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> ONCE. I BELIEVE I CALLED ON THE 3RD OF -- IN THE LATER MORNING, BEFORE THE AFTERNOON.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. HAD SOMEONE ALREADY PREARRANGED A TIME WHEN THE TWO OF YOU WOULD SPEAK?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NOT THAT I RECALL. I JUST MADE MY PHONE CALL.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. AND HE PICKED UP THE TELEPHONE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES. NICOLE SIMPSON PICKED UP THE PHONE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DID YOU NEXT SPEAK TO THE DEFENDANT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> AFTER I SPOKE WITH NICOLE, YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. AND DID YOU RECOGNIZE THE DEFENDANT'S VOICE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WAS IT A VOICE YOU HEARD BEFORE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WHERE HAD YOU HEARD THE DEFENDANT'S VOICE BEFORE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NUMEROUS TIMES ON TELEVISION.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DID YOU ASK THE DEFENDANT ABOUT THE OCCURRENCES OF JANUARY 1, 1989?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND WHAT DID HE SAY?
<P>
<B>A:</B> HE EXPLAINED TO ME THAT AFTER HE AND NICOLE RETURNED HOME AFTER A NEW YEAR'S EVE PARTY, THAT THEY WERE READY -- THEY WERE IN THEIR BEDROOM AND A VERBAL DISPUTE BROKE OUT BETWEEN THEM AND THAT THE DISPUTE GOT OUT OF HAND AND IT BECAME PHYSICAL. HE TOLD ME THAT IT TURNED INTO A MUTUAL TYPE WRESTLING MATCH AND THAT WAS BASICALLY IT; NOTHING MORE THAN THAT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU ASK THE DEFENDANT ABOUT THE INJURIES NICOLE BROWN SUSTAINED?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YEAH. I ASKED HIM ABOUT THE -- BECAUSE I HAD A PHOTOGRAPH THAT SHOWED INJURY TO HER FOREHEAD, AND I TOLD HIM THAT I LOOKED AT A PHOTOGRAPH THAT DEPICTED SOME INJURY TO NICOLE'S FOREHEAD AND HE SAID, "WELL, I KNOW. I WAS SURPRISED TO EVEN SEE THAT IT HAD OCCURRED BECAUSE OF THE INCIDENT."
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID HE DENY CAUSING THOSE INJURIES?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO, HE DID NOT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID HE ADMIT CAUSING THOSE INJURIES?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, HE DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU ASK THE DEFENDANT ABOUT THE 911 CALL TO THE POLICE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO, I DON'T THINK I ASKED HIM ANYTHING ABOUT THE PHONE CALL ITSELF, NO.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. SO BASICALLY THEN ALL YOU ASKED HIM WAS WHAT HAPPENED?
<P>
<B>A:</B> THAT'S CORRECT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> NOW, AFTER RECEIVING THIS INFORMATION FROM THE DEFENDANT, DID YOU WRITE A REPORT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU INCLUDE IN THAT REPORT THE INFORMATION THE DEFENDANT GAVE YOU?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU CONTINUE TO INVESTIGATE THE MATTER?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID. I ASKED -- AFTER I DID THE INITIAL TELEPHONE INTERVIEW WITH THE DEFENDANT AND NICOLE, I TOLD NICOLE THAT I WOULD LIKE TO SEE HER IN PERSON, IF SHE CAN MAKE ARRANGEMENTS TO COME TO THE POLICE STATION. SHE AGREED AND SAID SHE WOULD COME DOWN THE NEXT DAY. SHE WOULD ALSO BRING HER TWO KIDS WITH HER, AND SHE DID COME DOWN AND MEET ME.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. AND SO YOU DID MEET NICOLE BROWN?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WHAT DAY WAS THAT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I BELIEVE THAT WAS THE 3RD -- THE 4TH, THE 4TH OF JANUARY, THE NEXT DAY.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY.
AND WHAT INJURIES, IF ANY, DID YOU NOTICE ON HER FACE AND NECK AND HEAD AREA AT THAT TIME?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I JUST NOTICED SOME BRUISING ON HER FOREHEAD. THAT WAS ALL.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> THE RECORD SHOULD REFLECT THE WITNESS INDICATED THE RIGHT SIDE OF THE FOREHEAD.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: AND DID YOU REINTERVIEW HER?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YEAH. I EXPLAINED TO HER WHAT WAS GOING TO HAPPEN IN THIS CASE AND I ASKED -- I EXPLAINED TO HER THE PROCEDURES THAT WOULD HAPPEN.
I REVIEWED THE ORIGINAL POLICE REPORT WITH HER AND ASKED HER TO REVIEW IT. WE REVIEWED IT TOGETHER.
I ASKED HER, "DOES THIS ACCURATELY DEPICT WHAT HAPPENED OVER THE WEEKEND?"
SHE SAID, "YES."
I SAID, "IS THIS YOUR SIGNATURE ON THE REPORT?"
SHE SAID, "YES, IT IS."
AND THEN I EXPLAINED THAT I WOULD BE PRETTY -- PREPARING THE CASE FOR A PROSECUTING ATTORNEY.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU REFER THE CASE TO THE L.A. CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DO THEY HAVE A SPECIAL UNIT THAT HANDLES CASES LIKE THESE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I BELIEVE THEY DO. I MET WITH THE SUPERVISING ATTORNEY THERE AND PROVIDED HER WITH THE INFORMATION.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND WHAT WAS THE SUPERVISING ATTORNEY'S NAME?
<P>
<B>A:</B> MARY CLARE MOLIDOR.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> YOU GAVE DEPUTY CITY ATTORNEY MOLIDOR ALL THE REPORTS?
<P>
<B>A:</B> THAT IS CORRECT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU SHOW HER THE PHOTOGRAPHS?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> HOW DO WE SPELL MOLIDOR?
<P>
<B>THE WITNESS:</B> I BELIEVE IT IS M-O-L-I-D-O-R.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> THANK YOU.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: DO YOU RECALL THE DATE IN WHICH YOU TURNED OVER YOUR CASE FILE TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I BELIEVE IT MAY HAVE BEEN THE AFTERNOON OF THE 4TH OR THE MORNING OF THE 5TH. I DO NOT RECALL THE EXACT TIME.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND AFTER YOU REFERRED THE MATTER OVER TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE, DID YOU AGAIN SPEAK WITH THE DEFENDANT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID. HE PHONED ME AT MY DESK EARLY IN THE AFTERNOON. I BELIEVE IT WAS AFTER LUNCH.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WAS THE CASE AGAINST THE DEFENDANT FILED?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, IT WAS.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WHAT WAS FILED?
<P>
<B>A:</B> ONE COUNT OF SPOUSAL BATTERY. I BELIEVE IT IS 273(A) OF THE PENAL CODE. I'M NOT EXACTLY SURE.
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> MAY I HAVE ONE MOMENT, YOUR HONOR?
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> SURE.
<P>
(DISCUSSION HELD OFF THE RECORD
BETWEEN THE DEPUTY DISTRICT
ATTORNEYS.)
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: WHEN YOU SPOKE TO THE DEFENDANT ON THE TELEPHONE, JANUARY 5 -- THAT CALL WAS JANUARY 5, CORRECT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> THAT IS CORRECT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WHEN YOU SPOKE TO HIM ON THE TELEPHONE ON JANUARY 5, WHAT DID HE SAY?
<P>
<B>A:</B> WELL, MR. SIMPSON PHONED ME AND HE WAS INQUIRING ABOUT WHAT HIS CASE STATUS WITH HIS INCIDENT WAS. I EXPLAINED TO HIM THAT I HAD TURNED OVER THE ENTIRE CASE FILE TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE AND A DECISION HAD NOT YET BEEN MADE AND MR. --
THE DEFENDANT AND I DID HAVE A CONVERSATION. HE DISCUSSED WITH ME HIS FEELINGS ABOUT THE MATTER. HE WANTED TO RELAY TO ME THAT HE WAS SORRY THAT THE POLICE HAD TO COME TO HIS RESIDENCE AND THAT ME AS A DETECTIVE HAD TO GET INVOLVED IN HIS PERSONAL PROBLEMS.
AND HE WAS REALLY REMORSEFUL ABOUT WHAT HAPPENED THAT DAY AND THAT HE AND NICOLE WERE SEEKING -- WERE GOING TO SEEK COUNSELING TO RESOLVE THEIR FAMILY PROBLEMS, AND THAT I -- IF I COULD RELAY THAT TO THE CITY ATTORNEY WHEN THEY MAKE THEIR FINAL DECISION IN FILING THE CASE.
I TOLD MR. SIMPSON I WOULD DO THAT, BUT I ALSO TOLD MR. SIMPSON THAT IT IS MOST LIKELY HE IS LOOKING AT A FILING FOR A CRIMINAL CHARGE AND THAT HE -- HE WOULD ONE DAY HAVE TO FACE UP TO WHAT HAPPENED AND WOULD HAVE TO ANSWER FOR IT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DO YOU RECALL HIM SAYING ANYTHING ELSE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO. THAT WAS -- IT WAS ACTUALLY A PLEASANT CONVERSATION. I DON'T RECALL ANYTHING ELSE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. DID YOU WRITE A REPORT IN THIS MATTER?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> I HAVE A REPORT HERE, YOUR HONOR, DATED FEBRUARY 8, 1989.
DO YOU HAVE IT?
<P>
(DISCUSSION HELD OFF THE RECORD
BETWEEN DEPUTY DISTRICT ATTORNEY
AND DEFENSE COUNSEL.)
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> ALL RIGHT. MR. DARDEN, YOU HAVE A REPORT?
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> YES, YOUR HONOR.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> FEBRUARY 8TH.
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> YES.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> '89.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: BEFORE I PROCEED WITH THE REPORT, DETECTIVE, DID THE DEFENDANT DESCRIBE FOR YOU OR MENTION TO YOU HOW NICOLE BROWN SUSTAINED THE INJURIES SHE SUSTAINED?
<P>
<B>A:</B> AGAIN, HE EXPLAINED THAT IT WAS A RESULT OF AN ARGUMENT THAT THEY HAD GOTTEN INTO THAT RESULTED IN A PHYSICAL ALTERCATION, MORE OF A MUTUAL TYPE WRESTLING MATCH AND NOTHING ELSE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DO YOU RECALL EVERYTHING THAT WAS SAID IN THE CONVERSATION?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I -- THAT IS THE MOST THAT I RECALL. UMM, IF I COULD LOOK -- IF I HAVE ANYTHING ELSE, I WOULD HAVE TO REFER TO THE REPORT.

<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> ALL RIGHT. DETECTIVE, IF YOU WOULD JUST READ THAT TO YOURSELF, PLEASE.
<P>
<B>THE WITNESS:</B> (WITNESS COMPLIES.)
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: HAVE YOU READ THE REPORT, DETECTIVE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DOES IT REFRESH YOUR RECOLLECTION?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, IT DOES.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> WHAT ELSE DID THE DEFENDANT SAY?
<P>
<B>A:</B> HE TOLD ME THAT HE WAS SORRY FOR WHAT HE DID TO NICOLE AND THAT HE DIDN'T MEAN TO HARM HER IN ANY WAY AND THAT HE WOULD SEEK COUNSELING WITH HER.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DIDN'T HE ALSO TELL YOU THAT HE KNEW WHAT HE DID WAS WRONG?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, HE DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> ISN'T THAT WHAT YOU WROTE IN YOUR REPORT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> NOW, WHEN HE TOLD YOU THAT HE DIDN'T MEAN TO HARM HIS WIFE, DID HE ELABORATE ON THAT AT ALL?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NOT THAT I RECALL.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> HE DIDN'T DESCRIBE THE INCIDENT AS A MUTUAL WRESTLING MATCH IN THIS JANUARY 5 CONVERSATION, DID HE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO, HE DID NOT.
<P>
(DISCUSSION HELD OFF THE RECORD
BETWEEN THE DEPUTY DISTRICT
ATTORNEYS.)
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: DID HE ASK YOU NOT TO FILE THE CASE?
<P>
<B>A:</B> HE ASKED ME TO RELAY HIS FEELINGS ABOUT THE WHOLE MATTER TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DID YOU DO THAT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> THE REPORT THAT YOU JUST READ DATED FEBRUARY 8, 1989, THAT REPORT WASN'T IN EXISTENCE WHEN YOU REFERRED THE MATTER TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE; IS THAT CORRECT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> NO. I, UMM, MAYBE NEED TO MAKE SOMETHING CLEAR ON THE REPORT. IT IS DATED 2/8/89. THAT MAY BE A TYPOGRAPHICAL ERROR.
THE CASE WAS FILED ON JANUARY 30, 1989. I MAY HAVE TYPED THE -- I TOOK THE STATEMENT THAT HE GAVE ME THAT SAME DAY AND I MAY HAVE PUT THE WRONG DATE ON THERE. IT SHOULD BE -- I BELIEVE IT IS 1/8/89.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY. BUT HE DID APOLOGIZE FOR HIS CONDUCT?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, HE DID. HE WAS VERY CORDIAL ABOUT IT.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> OKAY.
NOW, AFTER YOU REFERRED THE MATTER TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE, DID THEY GIVE YOU ANY FURTHER DIRECTIONS?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES. AFTER, UMM, SOME TIME, THEY ASKED ME TO LOOK INTO THE OTHER INCIDENTS THAT WERE DESCRIBED BY NICOLE. SHE APPARENTLY TOLD THE OFFICERS WHO WERE RESPONDING TO HER HOME THAT THE POLICE HAD BEEN OUT THERE ON NUMEROUS OTHER TIMES AND THEY ASKED ME TO LOOK INTO THAT SITUATION.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> AND DID YOU LOOK INTO THAT SITUATION?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> DID YOU DETERMINE THAT THERE WERE OTHER SITUATIONS OR OCCASIONS WHEN LAPD OFFICERS WENT TO 360 NORTH ROCKINGHAM?
<P>
<B>A:</B> YES, I DID. I INQUIRED WITH SOME OF THE MORE SENIOR OFFICERS AT WEST L.A. THAT HAD BEEN WORKING THE DIVISION FOR OVER THE LAST FIVE YEARS.
<P>
<B>MR. COCHRAN:</B> YOUR HONOR, I WOULD LIKE TO OBJECT, NOT TOTALLY RESPONSIVE. "INQUIRED" MAY TEND TO BE HEARSAY. I AM NOT SURE OF THE RESPONSE AT THIS POINT.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> SUSTAINED.
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> WHAT QUESTION?
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> THE QUESTION IS JUST A LITTLE OVERBROAD.
<P>
<B>Q:</B> BY MR. DARDEN: WHAT ACTION, IF ANY, DID YOU TAKE TO DETERMINE WHETHER OR NOT OTHER POLICE UNITS OR OFFICERS HAD GONE TO ROCKINGHAM?
<P>
<B>A:</B> I SPOKE WITH SENIOR OFFICERS AT WEST L.A. AND ASKED THEM IF THEY HAD EVER BEEN TO THE LOCATION ON ROCKINGHAM IN THE PAST.

ALL RIGHT.
MR. DOUGLAS, YOU HAD SOMETHING YOU WANTED TO BRING TO THE COURT'S ATTENTION BEFORE WE INVITE THE JURY TO JOIN US?
<P>
<B>MR. DOUGLAS:</B> I DID, YOUR HONOR.
THERE WAS A LETTER THAT WAS TRANSMITTED TO THE COURT AND A COPY GIVEN TO COUNSEL CONCERNING OUR SUPREME INTEREST IN QUICKLY EXAMINING ITEMS OF PHYSICAL EVIDENCE.
AS THE COURT IS AWARE, THE PEOPLE HAVE APPARENTLY NOW CONCLUDED THEIR TESTING ON ITEMS OF EVIDENCE. THERE HAVE BEEN DISCUSSIONS FROM MR. BLASIER, MR. SCHECK ALONG WITH MR. CLARK AND MR. HARMON, AND THERE HAS BEEN AN AGREEMENT THAT THE ITEMS MAY BE SHIPPED TO THE FORENSICS LABORATORY IN ALBANY, NEW YORK, OF DR. BARBARA WOLF, ONE OF OUR DOCTORS.
WE HAVE NOT IN EARLIER OCCASIONS HAD A CHANCE TO PHYSICALLY TOUCH ANY OF THE ITEMS OF EVIDENCE, ANY OF THE SEROLOGICAL EVIDENCE MIND YOU. WE HAD NOT HAD A CHANCE TO TAKE OUR OWN PICTURES.
<P>
WE WERE HOPING THAT THIS CAN BE DONE SOON AND WE WERE SEEKING TO INTRODUCE THE PROTOCOL CONSISTENT WITH THAT WHICH WAS USED WITH CELLMARK SO THAT THEY WOULD BE ALLOWED TO HAVE A REPRESENTATIVE PRESENT FOR CHAIN OF CUSTODY MATTERS.
THEY WOULD BE ALLOWED TO OBSERVE THE CUTTING OR THE SPLITTING OF ANY SAMPLES. HOWEVER, THEY WOULD NOT BE ALLOWED TO WATCH THE ACTUAL TESTING SO THAT WE CAN MAINTAIN THE INTEGRITY OF OUR TESTING METHODOLOGIES.
I WANTED TO TRY TO GET SOME SORT OF CLOSURE ON THIS ISSUE SO THAT WE MAY QUICKLY BE ABLE TO GET THE ITEMS TAKEN BACK, TESTED AND THEN RETURNED BEFORE THEY BE USED IN THIS ACTUAL TRIAL. GIVEN THAT WE ARE CURRENTLY ON THE DOMESTIC DISCORD ASPECT OF THE TRIAL WHERE THE PHYSICAL EVIDENCE IS LESS PROBATIVE OR EVEN NECESSARY, I WAS HOPEFUL THAT I COULD FASHION SOME RESOLUTION TODAY SO THAT WE HAVE THOSE ITEMS SENT OUT IN THE COMING DAYS.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> MISS CLARK.
<P>
<B>MS. CLARK:</B> YES.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> I DID RECEIVE A PHOTOCOPY OF A FAX LETTER AND I DON'T RECALL -- HOWEVER, THAT WAS EARLY IN THE MORNING AS WE WERE TRYING TO DEAL WITH OTHER MATTERS.
MISS CLARK.
<P>
<B>MS. CLARK:</B> YES, YOUR HONOR.
<P>
I SPOKE TO MR. DOUGLAS THIS AFTERNOON AND HE INFORMED ME AT A QUARTER TO 3:00 THAT HE WANTED TO ADDRESS THIS MATTER AT 3:15. I CALLED UPSTAIRS TO FIND OUT IF I COULD GET ROCK AND WOODY HERE BECAUSE THEY DID HAVE VERY SPECIFIC REQUESTS ABOUT THE PROCEDURES THEY WANTED TO HAVE EMPLOYED.
UNFORTUNATELY, THEY ARE AT SID. THEY WILL NOT BE ABLE TO MAKE IT UNTIL TOMORROW. HOWEVER, I ASKED THAT THEY BE AVAILABLE FIRST THING IN THE MORNING TOMORROW TO ADDRESS IT.

<B>THE COURT:</B> ALL RIGHT.

<B>Q:</B> CERTAINLY, SIR.
PRIOR TO MR. SIMPSON ENTERING A PLEA TO THIS MISDEMEANOR CHARGE OF 273.5 P.C., DID MISS NICOLE BROWN SIMPSON INDICATE A DESIRE TO DROP ALL CHARGES AGAINST HER HUSBAND AND HAVE A CITY ATTORNEY HEARING?
<P>
<B>A:</B> WELL, WHEN I FIRST MET HER ON THE 4TH, SHE BROUGHT THE KIDS WITH HER AND I DISCUSSED WHAT HAPPENS WITH THESE TYPE OF CASES, AND I WANTED HER INPUT ABOUT HER FEELINGS TOWARDS PROSECUTION. AT THAT TIME, SHE SAID IF SHE COULD AVOID IT, SHE DOESN'T WANT TO PROSECUTE.
BUT I TOLD HER THAT NO MATTER WHAT SHE TOLD ME, EVEN THOUGH SHE DIDN'T WANT TO PROSECUTE, I WOULD HAVE TO TAKE THE CASE TO THE CITY ATTORNEY'S OFFICE. THEN I DISCUSSED SOME OF THE OPTIONS THAT THE CITY ATTORNEY MAY DO, AND ONE OF THOSE IS THE CITY ATTORNEY HEARING. AND THEN AT THAT TIME, SHE SAID, "WELL, I WOULD LIKE TO HAVE THAT. <P>
MR. SHAPIRO SAID, "WELL, MY CLIENT IS VERY HEAVILY MEDICATED AND I REALLY DON'T KNOW IF IT WOULD BE APPROPRIATE TO BRING HIM IN." AND THEN DAVID SUGGESTED THAT HE EASE HIM OFF THE MEDICATION SO THAT HE COULD COME IN FOR FURTHER QUESTIONING, AND MR. SHAPIRO SAID, "NO, I DON'T KNOW ABOUT THAT. I'LL GET BACK TO YOU," AND THEN HE NEVER DID.
<P>
<B>MR. SHAPIRO:</B> NO, THAT'S NOT TRUE.
WHAT I SAID TO MR. CONN WAS PRETTY CLEAR.
THE FINAL THING -- YOU'LL SEE IT IN THE LETTER -- I SAID THE CONDITION WOULD BE THAT BOTH SIDES WOULD STIPULATE THAT IT IS ADMISSIBLE, AND MR. CONN SAID, "WE CAN'T DO THAT. THAT'S AGAINST THE POLICY."
MY LETTER SPECIFICALLY AS I RECALL -- I HAVEN'T SEEN THIS LETTER IN MONTHS, BUT IN MY LETTER, I SAID HE WOULD CONSIDER IT IF THE RESULTS WOULD BE ADMISSIBLE.
<P>
<B>MS. CLARK:</B> BUT OUR CONVERSATION CAME AFTER THAT LETTER. THAT'S THE POINT. BUT --
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> BUT YOU ARE GOING TO OFFER THIS STATEMENT WITHOUT ANY REFERENCE TO POLYGRAPH?
<P>
<B>MS. CLARK:</B> RIGHT. RIGHT. THAT WAS OUR INTENT.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> OKAY.
<P>
<B>MR. DOUGLAS:</B> IT HAMPERS MY ABILITY TO CROSS-EXAMINE.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> I UNDERSTAND.
<P>
(THE FOLLOWING PROCEEDINGS WERE
HELD IN OPEN COURT:)
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> ALL RIGHT.
BACK ON THE RECORD.
MR. COCHRAN.
<P>
<B>MR. COCHRAN:</B> YES, YOUR HONOR.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> HAVE YOU HAD THE OPPORTUNITY TO TALK TO YOUR CLIENT ABOUT RONALD SHIPP?
<P>
<B>MR. COCHRAN:</B> YES, I HAVE, YOUR HONOR. HE HAS BEEN AWARE OF IT FOR SOME TIME. SO HE IS AWARE OF THAT.
MAYBE I SHOULD JUST STATE FOR THE RECORD --
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> CERTAINLY, PLEASE.
<P>
<B>MR. COCHRAN:</B> -- THE SITUATION.
YOUR HONOR, I UNDERSTAND THAT THE NEXT PEOPLE'S WITNESS IS MR. RONALD SHIPP, AND MR. SHIPP IS RELATED TO ME. HE IS A COUSIN. HIS FATHER IS THE FATHER OF MY COUSINS. HE HAS A DIFFERENT MOTHER.
AND I SHARED THAT WITH MR. SIMPSON. AND AS SUCH, THERE'S A POTENTIAL CONFLICT, BUT I'VE SHARED THAT WITH MR. SIMPSON AND HE WAIVES THAT CONFLICT. BECAUSE OF THE POTENTIAL RELATIONSHIP, I WILL NOT QUESTION THIS PARTICULAR WITNESS HOWEVER.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> ALL RIGHT.
MR. SIMPSON, IS THIS AGREEABLE TO YOU, THAT YOU HAVE NO OBJECTION TO MR. COCHRAN REMAINING AS YOUR COUNSEL DESPITE THE FACT THE PROSECUTION WILL BE CALLING A RELATIVE OF HIS AS A WITNESS?
<P>
<B>THE DEFENDANT:</B> YES. IT'S NO PROBLEM, YOUR HONOR.
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> THANK YOU.
ALL RIGHT.
COUNSEL, YOU'VE BROACHED AN INTERESTING LEGAL ISSUE THAT I HAVE NO IDEA WHAT'S COMING AGAIN. THANK YOU. WE ARE WITHIN 10 MINUTES OF THE END OF THE BUSINESS DAY IN ANY EVENT.
COUNSEL, IF YOU HAVE ANY CASES ON THE ISSUE, FAX THEM TO THE COURT AND I WILL PICK THEM UP TOMORROW MORNING. I WILL BE IN THE BUILDING TILL AROUND 6:00.
ANYTHING ELSE, COUNSEL?
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> WHAT TIME DO WE ADJOURN TOMORROW?
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> 9:00 O'CLOCK.
<P>
<B>MR. DARDEN:</B> NOT BEGIN. ADJOURN. 4:00 O'CLOCK OR 3:30?
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> 4:00 O'CLOCK.
<P>
<B>MS. CLARK:</B> WHEN IS THE 3:30 DAY?
<P>
<B>THE COURT:</B> THAT WAS THE DAY THE JUROR HAD TO GO TO A DOCTOR'S APPOINTMENT AT THE END OF THE DAY.
WE'LL STAND IN RECESS UNTIL 9:00 O'CLOCK.
<P>
(AT 4:25 P.M., AN ADJOURNMENT
WAS TAKEN UNTIL, WEDNESDAY,
FEBRUARY 1, 1995, 9:00 A.M.)
